# Debt Protocol · Chapter 1 · Wake Into Debt

**File:** `media/novel/ch01-pNN.png` (match `NN` to panel id, e.g. `novel-p12` → `ch01-p12.png`).

## How to use these prompts
1. Copy the **Full prompt** for one panel into your image model as the **scene + art direction** positive (action, environment, lighting intent, readability, and framing).
2. Add **rendering medium and look** yourself—brush style, film grain, painterly vs clean line, palette, and any extra “no text” reinforcement—in a preset or a second positive block.
3. Match aspect ratio to **Layout** (wide splash vs tall tier).
4. Keep speech balloons off the render if you composite them in post; the site supplies balloon text separately.

---

## novel-p1 · page 1 · span-12

**Layout:** wide splash (~2:1 landscape). One strong establishing image; leave lower third relatively open for balloon overlay in post.

**Beat / copy (for you, not necessarily on the art):**

```
Max woke up mid-scream. He did not remember starting it. He only remembered being inside it, throat on fire, lungs trying to punch his way out.
```

**Full prompt (paste into generator as one block):**

Comic book panel. Balloon/caption intent: "Max woke up mid-scream. He did not remember starting it. He only remembered being inside it, throat on fire, lungs trying to punch his way out." Max — match Book 1 ref: Black male, warm brown skin, light blue zip onesie, large dark eyes, soft afro; never default to white features. Setting: same Book 1 cryo orientation bay as neighboring panels—pods, open gel pod, helper bot + EV suit stack, ribbed deck, vapor;… Leave balloon margin; do not paint yellow caption/dialogue into the art. Layout: wide splash.

**Tracking (for filenames / sheets, not part of the image prompt):**

Chapter 1, Wake Into Debt, panel 1, comic page 1

---

## novel-p25 · page 16 · span-6 · UI readout

**Layout:** vertical tier panel (~4:5 portrait). Tight readable focal; leave margin for balloon overlay in post.

**Beat / copy (for you, not necessarily on the art):**

```
THE BLUE UI ERUPTED / HUD readout: [CORE ATTRIBUTES DETECTED]
EFFICIENCY 11
LUCK 06
TECHNICAL 12
SPEED 09
LEVEL 1

[NEW RULESET APPLIED]
World interactions now mediated by licensed nanotechnology.
```

**Full prompt (paste into generator as one block):**

Comic book panel. FPV: cyan HUD sheets rush toward camera; legible attribute readout in-art: "[CORE ATTRIBUTES DETECTED] EFFICIENCY 11 LUCK 06 TECHNICAL 12 SPEED 09 LEVEL 1 [NEW RULESET APPLIED] World interactions now mediated by licensed nanotechnology." Hands/forearms at bottom/sides, cyan rim light—match other Ch.1 first-person UI refs. No full body, no wide bay. THE BLUE UI ERUPTED is typeset in the yellow caption only, not painted. Tall ~4:5; HUD dominates. Leave balloon margin; do not paint yellow caption/dialogue into the art.

**Tracking (for filenames / sheets, not part of the image prompt):**

Chapter 1, Wake Into Debt, panel 25, comic page 16

```
People flowed around him, shoulders, carts, muttered apologies that weren't apologies, and for a second he was back in a life that still had weekends, watching someone click ignore on an alarm because downtime cost more than risk. The parallel was obscene. It arrived anyway.
```
